        var cookiePattern = new RegExp('(^|;)[ ]*' + cookieName + '=([^;]*)'),
            cookieMatch = cookiePattern.exec(document.cookie);
        return cookieMatch ? decodeURIComponent(cookieMatch[2]) : '';
    }

    <script type="text/javascript">
        function getBannerCookie(name){
            let cookie_start = document.cookie.indexOf(name);
            let cookie_end = document.cookie.indexOf(';', cookie_start);
            return cookie_start == -1 ? '' : decodeURIComponent(document.cookie.substring(cookie_start + name.length + 1, (cookie_end > cookie_start ? cookie_end : document.cookie.length)));
        }

        var bannerData = banner_ad_data;
        var bannerCounter = getBannerCookie('bannerCounter');
        if(bannerCounter !== '') {
        bannerCounter = JSON.parse(bannerCounter);
        }

        if(bannerCounter !== '' && bannerData[0][bannerCounter[0].number] !== undefined) {
        //  如果本条数据的计数未超过后台设置的上限值，则继续显示本条
                    if(bannerCounter[0].surplus < bannerData[0][bannerCounter[0].number].multi_show_num) {
                        $('.J_slick-pic0').attr('href', bannerData[0][bannerCounter[0].number].banner_ad_href).find('img').attr('src', bannerData[0][bannerCounter[0].number].banner_ad_img);
                    } else {

                        //  如果超过了上限并且同集中存在下一条数据，就取同集中的下一条数据
                        if(bannerCounter[0].number < bannerData[0].length - 1) {
        
                            $('.J_slick-pic0').attr('href', bannerData[0][bannerCounter[0].number+1].banner_ad_href).find('img').attr('src', bannerData[0][bannerCounter[0].number+1].banner_ad_img);
                        } else {
                            $('.J_slick-pic0').attr('href', bannerData[0][0].banner_ad_href).find('img').attr('src', bannerData[0][0].banner_ad_img);
                        }
                    }
        } else {
            $('.J_slick-pic0').attr('href', bannerData[0][0].banner_ad_href).find('img').attr('src', bannerData[0][0].banner_ad_img);
        }
    </script>
